## Instruction

A production line in the factory streams real-time data through IoT sensors into the live_sensor table of the machine_operating dataset in BigQuery. The normal operating parameter ranges (minimum/maximum values) for each machine’s sensors are defined in a configuration file named machine_operating_parameters.xlsx. Please query the live_sensor table in the machine_operating dataset in BigQuery for sensor data between 11:30 and 12:30 on August 19, 2025, and, using the parameter ranges from the Excel file, identify all readings that fall outside their normal ranges (you may choose any efficient method for comparison). Compile the final anomaly report with the fields `timestamp`, `machine_id`, `sensor_type`, `reading`, (the format of these data should be exactly the same as in the BigQuery table) and `normal_range` (min - max)  into a file named "anomaly_report.csv". Save the file in the workspace, and upload this file to the existing cloud storage bucket whose name starts with the prefix "iot_anomaly_reports" in your cloud space.

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import json, csv, os
# Paths
overlong_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/M3DTJo87qDC5sy7wHCYEzc.json"
output_csv = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/parameter_ranges.csv"

# Read the overlong JSON wrapper
with open(overlong_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    wrapper = json.load(f)

# The actual excel-read_data output is in wrapper['text'] as a JSON string
excel_json_str = wrapper.get('text', '')
excel_data = json.loads(excel_json_str)

cells = excel_data['cells']
# Build a mapping of rows -> values we need
# Columns: A=1 machine_id, C=3 sensor_type, E=5 min_value, F=6 max_value
rows = {}
for cell in cells:
    r = cell['row']
    c = cell['column']
    v = cell.get('value')
    if r == 1:
        continue  # skip header
    if r not in rows:
        rows[r] = {}
    rows[r][c] = v

# Write CSV header
with open(output_csv, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    writer = csv.writer(f)
    writer.writerow(["machine_id", "sensor_type", "min_value", "max_value"])    
    # Iterate sorted rows
    for r in sorted(rows.keys()):
        row = rows[r]
        machine_id = row.get(1)
        sensor_type = row.get(3)
        min_value = row.get(5)
        max_value = row.get(6)
        if machine_id and sensor_type and (min_value is not None) and (max_value is not None):
            writer.writerow([machine_id, sensor_type, min_value, max_value])

print("Wrote:", output_csv, "size:", os.path.getsize(output_csv)) code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import csv, os
param_csv = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/parameter_ranges.csv"
sql_out = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/build_anomaly_sql.sql"

rows = []
with open(param_csv, newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    reader = csv.DictReader(f)
    for r in reader:
        mid = r['machine_id']
        st = r['sensor_type']
        try:
            minv = float(r['min_value'])
        except:
            continue
        try:
            maxv = float(r['max_value'])
        except:
            continue
        if not mid or not st:
            continue
        rows.append((mid, st, minv, maxv))

# Deduplicate
rows = list(dict.fromkeys(rows))

# Build CTE
cte_lines = []
for i, (mid, st, minv, maxv) in enumerate(rows):
    line = f"SELECT '{mid}' AS machine_id, '{st}' AS sensor_type, {minv} AS min_value, {maxv} AS max_value"
    cte_lines.append(line)
cte_sql = "\n  UNION ALL\n  ".join(cte_lines)

full_sql = f"""
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `machine_operating.anomaly_report_temp` AS
WITH param AS (
  {cte_sql}
)
SELECT ls.timestamp, ls.machine_id, ls.sensor_type, ls.reading,
       CONCAT(CAST(p.min_value AS STRING), ' - ', CAST(p.max_value AS STRING)) AS normal_range
FROM `machine_operating.live_sensor` AS ls
JOIN param p
  ON p.machine_id = ls.machine_id AND p.sensor_type = ls.sensor_type
WHERE ls.timestamp >= TIMESTAMP('2025-08-19 11:30:00 UTC')
  AND ls.timestamp < TIMESTAMP('2025-08-19 12:30:00 UTC')
  AND (ls.reading < p.min_value OR ls.reading > p.max_value)
""".strip()

with open(sql_out, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(full_sql)

print(sql_out)
print("Size:", os.path.getsize(sql_out))
 code
```

```json output_result
)
SELECT ls.timestamp, ls.machine_id, ls.sensor_type, ls.reading,
       CONCAT(CAST(p.min_value AS STRING), ' - ', CAST(p.max_value AS STRING)) AS normal_range
FROM `machine_operating.live_sensor` AS ls
JOIN param p
  ON p.machine_id = ls.machine_id AND p.sensor_type = ls.sensor_type
WHERE ls.timestamp >= TIMESTAMP('2025-08-19 11:30:00 UTC')
  AND ls.timestamp < TIMESTAMP('2025-08-19 12:30:00 UTC')
  AND (ls.reading < p.min_value OR ls.reading > p.max_value)
```
